i > 0; --i) {\n    24→    if (bset[i - 1]) {\n    25→      return i;\n    26→    }\n    27→  }\n    28→  return 0;  // All zeros\n    29→}\n    30→\n    31→template <typename KeyType>\n    32→auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {\n    33→  if (n_bits_ <= 0) {\n    34→    return;\n    35→  }\n    36→\n    37→  std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);\n    38→\n    39→  // Calculate hash of the element\n    40→  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);\n    41→\n    42→  // Extract the first n_bits to determine bucket index\n    43→  uint32_t bucket_idx = hash & ((1U << n_bits_) - 1);\n    44→\n    45→  // Shift hash right by n_bits to get the remaining bits\n    46→  hash_t remaining_bits = hash >> n_bits_;\n    47→\n    48→  // Compute binary representation of remaining bits\n    49→  std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> bset = ComputeBinary(remaining_bits);\n    50→\n    51→  // Find position of leftmost one bit\n    52→  uint64_t position = PositionOfLeftmostOne(bset);\n    53→\n    54→  // Update register with maximum position\n    55→  if (position > registers_[bucket_idx]) {\n    56→    registers_[bucket_idx] = position;\n    57→  }\n    58→}\n    59→\n    60→template <typename KeyType>\n    61→auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {\n    62→  std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);\n    63→\n    64→  if (n_bits_ <= 0) {\n    65→    cardinality_ = 0;\n    66→    return;\n    67→  }\n    68→\n    69→  // Calculate the raw estimate using harmonic mean\n    70→  double raw_estimate = 0.0;\n    71→  for (uint32_t i = 0;
